============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK18)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A**c1 + c2*_p*sin(c3*A)
Candidate formulas: 60

GT is the fixed function (independent of `t`):
\[
f(A)= -0.5637231318832533\,A^2 + 0.1313786441969526\,\sin(0.7616913890711074\,A).
\]
So any matching candidate must (i) be independent of `t` after parameter choices, (ii) have exactly an \(A^2\) polynomial term with coefficient \(-0.5637...\), (iii) have exactly one sine term of the form \(K\sin(\omega A)\) with **no phase shift** (GT has 0 shift), and (iv) have no extra terms (constants, linear in \(A\), logs, exps, Max/Abs artifacts, etc.) unless they can be set to 0 identically.

Below, for each candidate, I check whether we can set its free constants to make it exactly \( -0.5637 A^2 + 0.1313786\sin(0.7616914 A)\) for all real \(A,t\).

---

### 1. `A**2*c0 + A*c1*(c2 + t)**c3 + c4*sin(A*c5 + c6) + c7`
Set `c1=0` to remove `t` term; set `c7=0`. Need `c0=-0.563723...`. Sine must have zero phase: set `c6=0`, `c4=0.1313786`, `c5=0.7616914`. Works. ✅ **Match possible**.

### 2. `A**2*c0/(A*c1 + c2) + A*c3*log(c4*exp(A*c5) + 1)/(A*c1 + c2) + A*c6/(A*c1 + c2)`
This is rational in \(A\) with logs/exp; cannot reduce to polynomial \(A^2\) plus pure sine for all \(A\). Denominator forces non-polynomial unless degenerate; but any degeneration (e.g., `c1=0`) still leaves \(A^2/c2\) (ok) but other terms are \(A\log(1+c4 e^{A c5})\) etc., not sine and cannot be identically zero unless coefficients 0. If set `c3=c6=0`, expression becomes \(A^2*c0/(A*c1+c2)\), not \(A^2\) unless `c1=0`, then it’s \((c0/c2)A^2\) but then no sine term. ❌

### 3. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*cos(A*c3) + A**c4*c5/(A**c4 + c6)`
Can set `c1=0`, `c2=0`, and last fraction to 0 by `c5=0`. Then only \(A^2 c0\) remains, missing sine. If keep cosine, cosine cannot become sine with zero phase for all \(A\) (cos is phase-shifted sine by \(\pi/2\), but there is no additive phase parameter inside cos). Also cosine term is multiplied by \(A\), unlike GT. ❌

### 4. `A**c0*c1 + c2*sin(A*c3 + c4)`
We can set exponent `c0=2` and `c1=-0.563723...` to get \(-0.5637 A^2\). For sine: need amplitude `c2=0.1313786`, frequency `c3=0.7616914`, and phase `c4=0`. Works. ✅

### 5. `c0*sin(A*c1 + c2) + c3*Max(0, A)**2`
`Max(0,A)^2` is 0 for \(A<0\) and \(A^2\) for \(A>0\); cannot equal \(-0.5637 A^2\) for all real \(A\) unless `c3=0`, but then no \(A^2\) term. ❌

### 6. `A**2*c0 + c1*sin(c2 + c3*Abs(A))`
Has `Abs(A)` inside sine; GT uses \(A\) (odd argument), not \(|A|\) (even). Cannot match for negative \(A\) unless sine term is identically 0, but then missing sine. ❌

### 7. `A**2*c0 + c1*sin(A*c2 + c3)`
Set `c0=-0.563723...`, `c1=0.1313786`, `c2=0.7616914`, `c3=0`. Exactly GT. ✅

### 8. `c0*Abs(A)**2 + c1*sin(A*c2 + c3)`

- A term proportional to sin(linear function of A) — specifically sin(c*A) with no phase shift needed (but phase shift can be set to 0)

Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `A²c0 + Ac1 + Ac2*cos(Ac3) + A^c4*c5/(A^c4+c6)`

**Candidate 4:** `A^c0 * c1 + c2*sin(Ac3+c4)`
